 Thil Production Shjring Contract (thii "Contract”) is between:                              <br /><br /><br />
 Ul The Kurdistan Regional Government of Iraq (the "Government'); and                        <br /><br /><br />
 (21 Hess Middle East New Ventures Limited, a company established and existing               <br /><br /><br />
 under the laws of the Cayman Islands, whose registered office is at Caledonian              <br /><br /><br />
 Trust (Cayman) Limited, Caledonian House, 69 Or. Roy's Drive, P.O. Box 1043,                <br /><br /><br />
 George Town, Grand Cayman. Cayman Islands KYI -1102; (''Hess*) and                          <br /><br /><br />
 (3| Petroceltic Kurdistan Limited, a limited liability company organized and                <br /><br /><br />
 existing under the laws of the British Virgin Islands under company number                  <br /><br /><br />
 1551655, whose registered office is at 3rd Floor. Windward House. La Route de la            <br /><br /><br />
 Liberation, St Helier, Jersey ('’PKL*')                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 (Hess and PKL together the ’Contractor* and each a ^Contractor Entity*).                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
Recitals                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
A.    The Government has determined that this Contract will facilitate the development of    <br /><br /><br />
the petroleum wealth of the Kurdistan Region in a way that achieves the highest benefit      <br /><br /><br />
to the people of the Kurdistan Region and all of Iraq, will promote the economic             <br /><br /><br />
development of the Kurdistan Region and Iraq and the social welfare of its people, uses      <br /><br /><br />
the most advanced techniques, and accesses best market principles to encourage               <br /><br /><br />
investment.                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
B.    The Government enters into this Contract pursuant to the Government's rights and       <br /><br /><br />
authorities under the Constitution of Iraq and the Kurdistan Oil and Gas Law 2007. In        <br /><br /><br />
accordance with the Constitution of Iraq, the prevailing Laws of the Kurdistan Region        <br /><br /><br />
comprise the Kurdistan Region Law and. with regard to a matter wholly within the             <br /><br /><br />
exclusive jurisdiction of the Government of Iraq, the federal Laws of Iraq.                  <br /><br /><br />
C.    Each Contractor Entity and the Government affirms its ongoing commitment and           <br /><br /><br />
adherence to the Principles and Criteria of the Extractive Industries Transparency           <br /><br /><br />
Initiative |EITI).                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
D.    Each Contractor Entity has assured the Government that such Contractor Entity has,     <br /><br /><br />
together with its Affiliates:                                                                <br /><br /><br />
(1)    the financial capability, and the technical knowledge and technical ability, to       <br /><br /><br />
carry out Petroleum Operations in the Contract Area under the terms of this                  <br /><br /><br />
Contract; and                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
(2)    a record of compliance with the principles of good corporate citizenship.             <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                                               Production Shoring Controct Dinorto  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
E. This Contract is a production sharing contract- The object of this Contract is for the           <br /><br /><br />
Contractor to undertake Petroleum Operations in the Contract Area at the Contractor's               <br /><br /><br />
sole risk and expense.                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
f. Neither the Contractor, nor any Contractor Entity will recerve any compensation for its          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
services, nor any reimbursement of its expenditures under this Contract, except for the             <br /><br /><br />
share of Petroleum from the Contract Area to which it may become entitled under this                <br /><br /><br />
Contract. If there is no Commerc-al Discovery in the Contract Area, or if the production            <br /><br /><br />
achieved from any Production Area is insufficient to reimburse the Contractor or any                <br /><br /><br />
Contractor Entity, each Contractor Entity will bear its own losses without any obligation           <br /><br /><br />
of the Government to provide any reimbursement or other compensation.                               <br /><br /><br />
G.    It is the policy of the Government to: (1) ensure that Natural Gas is first made available    <br /><br /><br />
to satisfy the consumption requirements and needs of the people of Iraq; (2) determine              <br /><br /><br />
and control all exports of Natural Gas produced in the Region; and (3) act, directly or             <br /><br /><br />
indirectly through a designated Affiliate of the Government or other designee of the                <br /><br /><br />
Government, as the aggregator of all Natural Gas produced in the Region for export.                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
H.    Nothing in this Contract is intended to confer any right upon the Contractor other than       <br /><br /><br />
those rights expressly granted in this Contract. This Contract does not transfer                    <br /><br /><br />
ownership of any Petroleum in the ground to the Contractor or any Contractor Entity.                <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
I.    Each Contractor Entity and its ultimate parent company have provided the Government           <br /><br /><br />
with a letter of representations and warranties dated on or before the date of this                 <br /><br /><br />
Contract (the "Letters of Representations") as an inducement for the Government to                  <br /><br /><br />
enter into this Contract, and upon each of which the Government is relying in entering              <br /><br /><br />
into this Contract.                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
J.    Concurrently with the signing of this Contract, Mess Corporation and Petroceltic              <br /><br /><br />
International PLC have delivered a guarantee in favour of the Government as required                <br /><br /><br />
by this Contract.                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
K.    Prior to this Contract. Hess and PKL delivered a Confidentiality and Pre Contractual          <br /><br /><br />
Understandings Agreement, which continues in accordance with its terms and is not                   <br /><br /><br />
impaired by this Contract, except as expressly set forth herein.                                    <br /><br /><br />

14.1 A4 used in this Contract:                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
’Approved Domestic Gas Marketing Work Program and Budget*’ is a Work Program for                                                           <br /><br /><br />
Domestic Gas Marketing Operations and associated Budget that has been approved by                                                          <br /><br /><br />
the Management Committee and the Government.                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
‘Approved Gas Field Appraisal Work Plan and Budget" means an Approved Work Plan                                                            <br /><br /><br />
and Budget for the Appraisal of a Gas Field.                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
'Domestic Gas Marketing Operations'* means Gas Marketing Operations solely in                                                              <br /><br /><br />
respect of the Domestic Market for Natural Gas. in all events carried out pursuant to and                                                  <br /><br /><br />
in accordance with an Approved Domestic Gas Marketing Work Program and Budget.                                                             <br /><br /><br />
'Domestic Gas Plan*' means a plan for the sale or other disposition of Natural Gas to the                                                  <br /><br /><br />
Domestic Market.                                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
'Domestic Market" means sales or other gas projects within the Region where the                                                            <br /><br /><br />
entirety of the Natural Gas is intended for consumption within Iraq.                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
'Export Gas Marketing Operations" means all Gas Marketing Operations in respect of                                                         <br /><br /><br />
an Export Market for Natural Gas.                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
'Export Market'' means sales of Natural Gas, including for transportation outside of the                                                   <br /><br /><br />
borders of Iraq, whether the deliveries or point of sale occur inside or outside the                                                       <br /><br /><br />
borders of Iraq where the ultimate destination of the volumes sold is outside of Iraq. A                                                   <br /><br /><br />
sale to the Government {whether directly or indirectly through a Public Company or                                                         <br /><br /><br />
other Affiliate of the Government designated by the Government) meeting the                                                                <br /><br /><br />
foregoing criteria will be within this definition.                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
'Gas Export Plan* means a plan for the sale or other disposition of Natural Gas to an                                                      <br /><br /><br />
Export Market, including a sale of Natural Gas to the Government, a Public Company or                                                      <br /><br /><br />
otherwise, in accordance with a gas sales and purchase agreement with the Contractor                                                       <br /><br /><br />
Entities, as proposed by the Government.                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
'Gas Marketing Operations* means any activity relating to the evaluation of markets or                                                     <br /><br /><br />
projects for the potential delivery, sale, processing, compression, and transportation of                                                  <br /><br /><br />
Natural Gas, including evaluations of potential markets and projects, the quantities of                                                    <br /><br /><br />
Natural Gas that could be sold, delivery specifications and requirements, production                                                       <br /><br /><br />
costs, transportation arrangements, and all other activities generally relevant to the                                                     <br /><br /><br />
identification of a sale or other disposition of Gas from the Contract Area, and includes                                                  <br /><br /><br />
such activities as they may relate to Gas from other Natural Gas producers in the Region.                                                  <br /><br /><br />
"Gas Marketing Operations* does not include the actual entry into any contract or                                                          <br /><br /><br />
contracts for the sale, dedication, designation, commitment, or other disposal of Gas                                                      <br /><br /><br />
from the Contract Area.                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />

duration; or                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />

with Kurdistan Region law, if such occupation will be long lasting or                               <br /><br /><br />
makes it henceforth impossible to resume original usage of such land                                <br /><br /><br />
or property.                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />

reasonable, in accordance with clause 29 of the Kurdistan Region Oil and Gas                        <br /><br /><br />
Law, and shall take into account the rights of the owner and any effective use                      <br /><br /><br />
of the land or property by its owner at the time of occupation by the                               <br /><br /><br />
Contractor.                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />

required pursuant to clause 29 of the Kurdistan Region Oil and Gas law) which                       <br /><br /><br />

 27.7    If any metering equipment is defective or not functioning property, the Contractor shall   <br /><br /><br />
 promptly notify the Government upon the discovery thereof and use all reasonable                   <br /><br /><br />
 endeavours to repair, adjust, correct, or replace it promptly (and in any event within 15          <br /><br /><br />
 days).                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 27.7.1    The "Adjustment Date** means the last date that the metering equipment was               <br /><br /><br />
 known or agreed to have been measuring correctly, or if not known or agreed,                       <br /><br /><br />
 the date that is midway between the date the defect was discovered and the                         <br /><br /><br />
 last date the equipment was known to have measured correctly.                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
 27.7.2    The results from the defectrve equipment shall be disregarded for the period             <br /><br /><br />
 from the Adjustment Date until the date the defective equipment is repaired or                     <br /><br /><br />
 replaced, and the measurement for such period shall be estimated:                                  <br /><br /><br />
 (a)    if check measuring equipment is installed and registering accurately,                       <br /><br /><br />
 then by using the measurements recorded by such check measuring                                    <br /><br /><br />
 equipment;                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
 (b)    if check measuring equipment is not installed or not registering                            <br /><br /><br />
 accurately, then by correcting the error if the percentage of error is                             <br /><br /><br />
 ascertainable by verification, calibration or mathematical calculation;                            <br /><br /><br />
 or                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
 (c)    if neither method set out in clause 27.7.2(a) or 27.7.2|b) is feasible,                     <br /><br /><br />
 then by estimating the volume or quantity delivered (or both) based                                <br /><br /><br />
 on deliveries during the preceding comparable period of time when                                  <br /><br /><br />
 the metering equipment was registering accurately.                                                 <br /><br /><br />

Month in which the due date for payments falls, as such average rate can be calculated            <br /><br /><br />
from the aforesaid daily rates of exchange published by the Central 8ank of Iraq.                 <br /><br /><br />
29.3    Any currency conversion to be made under this Contract shall be at the exchange rate of   <br /><br /><br />
the Central Bank of Iraq, provided such exchange rate applied to the Contractor Entities          <br /><br /><br />
shall not be less favourable than the rate offered by other private, commercial or                <br /><br /><br />
industrial banks in the international market. In the absence of the Central Bank of Iraq          <br /><br /><br />
or in the event that the Central Bank of Iraq is unable to provide the relevant exchange          <br /><br /><br />
rate, any currency conversion to be made under this Contract shall be at the exchange             <br /><br /><br />
rate of a reputable commercial bank carrying on business in the international market              <br /><br /><br />
and approved by the Parties.                                                                      <br /><br /><br />

Barrels of Crude Oil and Natural Gas BOE.                                                         <br /><br /><br />

Payments in full plus interest at the Agreed Rate within such 30-day cure                             <br /><br /><br />
period, the Government shall not exercise its lifting rights under clause 32.11 in                    <br /><br /><br />
respect of such defaulting Contractor Entity.                                                         <br /><br /><br />
32.12.2    In the case of any subsequent default by the same defaulting Contractor Entity,            <br /><br /><br />
the Government may exercise its right to lift, whether or not the defaulting                          <br /><br /><br />
Contractor Entity cures its default within the 30-day cure period or otherwise.                       <br /><br /><br />

produced under this Contract.                                                                       <br /><br /><br />

clause 33.2, the Contractor shall submit the following information to the Management                <br /><br /><br />
Committee in respect of any pipeline project:                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(a)    proposed pipeline route and related facilities;                                              <br /><br /><br />
(b)    forecasted pipeline flow rate and capacity;                                                  <br /><br /><br />
(c)    estimated capital costs and operating costs of the pipeline and related facilities;          <br /><br /><br />
(d)    proposed financing schedule;                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
(e)    construction schedule;                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(f)    general technical description of the pipeline and related facilities;                        <br /><br /><br />
(g)    construction plans and tests;                                                                <br /><br /><br />
(h)    preventive measures for damage to the environment and third parties; and                     <br /><br /><br />
(i)    any other information relating to the pipeline project.                                      <br /><br /><br />
The Management Committee shall examine all the above information and shall, within                  <br /><br /><br />
90 days, approve or disapprove the proposed pipeline project.                                       <br /><br /><br />
33.4    Subject to available capacity, tie-in agreements, and pipeline crude oil minimum quality    <br /><br /><br />
specifications, the Contractor shall permit third parties to transport their Petroleum              <br /><br /><br />

between the Contractor and such third party.                                                        <br /><br /><br />
ss.4.1 Such terms must be reasonable commercial terms and must not discriminate                     <br /><br /><br />
among potential third party users.                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
ss.4.2 The Contractor and the Government shall always have priority of access to such               <br /><br /><br />
pipelines.                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />

Clause 37 - Environmental; Worker Safety and Health                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />

GtfttftAl                                                                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
37.1 The Contractor shall carry out Petroleum Operations, and procure that they are carried                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
out, in such a manner as to:                                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
(a)    protect the natural environment and ensure that Petroleum Operations result                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
in minimum ecological damage or destruction;                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
(b)    ensure the safety, health and welfare of Persons in or affected by Petroleum                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
Operations;                                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(c)    manage the resources in a way which has long-term benefits to the Kurdistan                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
Region and the Contractor;                                                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(d)    maintain in safe and good condition and repair, the Contract Area and all                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
structures, facilities, installations, equipment and other property, and other                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
works, used or to be used in Petroleum Operations;                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
(e)    on the earlier of: (i) the termination of this Contract; and {ii) when no longer                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
required for Petroleum Operations; and. in either case, except with the consent                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
of the Government; or unless this Contract otherwise provides, abandon,                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
decommission, remove or dispose of the property and other works mentioned                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
in paragraph |d). clean up the Contract Area and make it good and safe, and                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
protect and restore the natural environment;                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
(f)    control the flow and prevent the waste or escape of Petroleum, water or any                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
product used in or derived by processing Petroleum;                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
(g| prevent the escape of any mixture of water or drilling fluid with Petroleum;                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
(h)    prevent damage to Petroleum-bearing strata in or outside the Contract Area;                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
(i)    except with the consent of the Government, keep separate each Reservoir                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
Discovered in the Contract Area, and such of the sources of water discovered in                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
the Contract Area as the Government directs;                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                         ai                                prevent water or any other matter entering any Reservoir through wells in the          <br /><br /><br />
                                                                           Contract Area, except when required by. and in accordance with, the                    <br /><br /><br />
                                         M                                 Development Plan and Best Practices and the EHS Standards;                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                           minimise interference with pre-existing rights and activities; and                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                         (I)    remedy in a timely fashion any damage caused to the natural environment.                                          <br /><br /><br />

 37.2 The Contractor shall implement a health, safety and environment program and take                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
 necessary measures to ensure hygiene, health and safety of its personnel carrying out                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
 Petroleum Operations in accordance with Best Practices (**EHS Standards**).                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
 37.3    The EHS Standards must be no less stringent than those set out in the relevant World                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 Bank Group Environmental, Health, and Safety Guidelines                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
 (http://www.ifc.orR/ifcext/sustainability.nsf/Content/EHSGuidelines).                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
 37.4                                                                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                         The measures the Contractor must take include the following:                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                         (a) supplying first aid and safety equipment for each work area and maintaining a                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                         healthy environment for personnel;                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                                          Production Shoring Controct Dinorto  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
(b)    reporting to the Government within 72 hours of such accident, any accident              <br /><br /><br />
where personnel has been injured while engaged in Petroleum Operations and                     <br /><br /><br />
resulting in such personnel being unable to return to work;                                    <br /><br /><br />
(c)    implementing a permit-to-work procedure around hazardous Assets and                     <br /><br /><br />
Materials and installations;                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
(d)    providing safe storage areas for explosives, detonators and any other                   <br /><br /><br />
dangerous products used in the operations;                                                     <br /><br /><br />
(e)    supplying fire extinguishing equipment in each work area;                               <br /><br /><br />
(f)    measures for the purpose of taking control of any blow out or fire which could          <br /><br /><br />
damage the environment or Petroleum Field, in accordance with Best Practices;                  <br /><br /><br />
and                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
(g| measures for the purpose of preventing any involuntary injection of fluids in              <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum formations and production of Crude Oil and Natural Gas at rates                      <br /><br /><br />
that do not conform to MER.                                                                    <br /><br /><br />

Decommissioning Plan and Buoget                                                             <br /><br /><br />
18.2    The Contractor shall undertake Decommissioning Operations in accordance with Best   <br /><br /><br />

the Contractor for the end of Commercial Production from each Production Area.              <br /><br /><br />

Decommissioning Plan within 90 days after receipt.                                          <br /><br /><br />
58.2.2    The Contractor's completion of Decommissioning Operations in accordance/ in       <br /><br /><br />
all material respects, with the Decommissioning Plan for a Production Area                  <br /><br /><br />
approved by the Management Committee and the Government will satisfy all                    <br /><br /><br />
of the Contractor's obligations with respect to the performance of                          <br /><br /><br />
Decommissioning Operations for such Production Area.                                        <br /><br /><br />
18.3    The Management Committee shall meet within 60 days following its receipt of         <br /><br /><br />
Contractor's proposal to examine and approve the Decommissioning Plan and Budget.           <br /><br /><br />
18.4    The Contractor shall not undertake Decommissioning Operations unless the            <br /><br /><br />
Government has approved the Decommissioning Plan and Work Program, and Budget.              <br /><br /><br />
18.5    The Contractor shall on the first anniversary of the submission of the first        <br /><br /><br />
Decommissioning Work Program and Budget and annually thereafter (or at such                 <br /><br /><br />
extended periods as may be agreed by the Government) during the term of this                <br /><br /><br />

Budgets taking into account changes in the Development Plan and advances in Best            <br /><br /><br />
Practices.                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
Decommissioning Reserve Fund                                                                <br /><br /><br />
18.6    To enable the Contractor to recover the costs associated with Decommissioning       <br /><br /><br />
Operations, the Contractor shall either establish a segregated fund to fund                 <br /><br /><br />

guarantees or bonds as the Government may require in accordance with Applicable Law.        <br /><br /><br />
58.6.1    The Decommissioning Reserve Fund must be established before the final 10          <br /><br /><br />
Calendar Years of the term of the Production Operations of a Production Area.               <br /><br /><br />
58.6.2    Once established, the Contractor shall make regular contributions to the          <br /><br /><br />
Decommissioning Reserve Fund based upon estimated decommissioning and                       <br /><br /><br />
site restoration costs in accordance with Best Practices.                                   <br /><br /><br />
58.6.3    The Contractor shall pay its contributions to the Decommissioning Reserve         <br /><br /><br />
Fund in US$.                                                                                <br /><br /><br />

Clause 40 - Force Majeure                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
DEFINITION                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
40.1 "Force Majeure" means any event: |1} that is unforeseeable, insurmountable, and                       <br /><br /><br />
irresistible, not caused by any error or omission by the Contractor acting as a reasonable                 <br /><br /><br />
and prudent operator and solely and directly caused by circumstances beyond the                            <br /><br /><br />
control of the Contractor as a reasonable and prudent operator; and (2) which prevents                     <br /><br /><br />
or impedes performance of all or part of the Contractor's obligations under this                           <br /><br /><br />
Contract. Such events include:                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(a)    war. whether declared or not. civil war. insurrection, riots, civil commotion,                      <br /><br /><br />
terrorism, any other hostile acts, whether internal or external;                                           <br /><br /><br />
(b)    strikes or other labour conflicts;                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
(c)    accidents or blowouts;                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
(d)    quarantine restrictions or epidemics;                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                      100                                                  <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                                                                             Production Shoring Controct Dinorto  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
 (e>                                        any act. event, happening or occurrence due to natural causes. in particular,         <br /><br /><br />
                                            but without limitation, floods, storms, cyclones, fires, lightning, earthquakes, or   <br /><br /><br />
 (0                                         lack of water necessary for Petroleum Operations; and                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                            any acts or orders of any competent foreign governmental authority validly            <br /><br /><br />
                                            asserting jurisdiction over the Contractor or a Contractor Entity.                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
EfftCT                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
40.2    No delay, default, breach or omission of the Contractor or a Contractor Entity »n the                                     <br /><br /><br />
performance of any of their respective obligations under this Contract will be considered                                         <br /><br /><br />
a material breach of this Contract if such delay, default, breach or omission is due to                                           <br /><br /><br />
Force Majeure.                                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
40.3    The Contractor shall promptly notify the Government of the occurrence of a Force                                          <br /><br /><br />
Majeure Event and take all reasonably appropriate measures to perform its obligations                                             <br /><br /><br />
under this Contract to the extent possible.                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
40.4    The time resulting from any such delay or curtailment in the execution of such                                            <br /><br /><br />
obligations, increased by the time necessary to repair any damage resulting from or                                               <br /><br /><br />
occurred during such delay or curtailment, shall be added to any time period provided                                             <br /><br /><br />
under this Contract (including the Exploration Period and any extension thereto, any                                              <br /><br /><br />
Sub-Period and any extension thereto and any Development Period and any extension                                                 <br /><br /><br />
thereto).                                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
40.5    The Government and the Contractor shall meet as soon as possible after the notification                                   <br /><br /><br />
of Force Majeure with a view to using reasonable endeavours to mitigate the effects                                               <br /><br /><br />
thereof.                                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
40.6    An event affecting a Contractor Entity will be considered Force Majeure affecting the                                     <br /><br /><br />
Contractor if the consequence of such Force Majeure prevents the performance of any                                               <br /><br /><br />
of the Contractor's obligations under this Contract. The application or potential                                                 <br /><br /><br />
application of any Law applicable to a Contractor Entity or any of its Affiliates, other                                          <br /><br /><br />
than Kurdistan Region Law or other Laws of the Republic of Iraq, which could result in a                                          <br /><br /><br />
criminal or civil penalty or sanction, is not Force Majeure.                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
40.7    The following events or circumstances will not constitute Force Majeure:                                                  <br /><br /><br />
(a)    any event or circumstance arising in connection with any Assets and Materials                                              <br /><br /><br />
or facilities other than the Assets and Materials and facilities of the Contractor                                                <br /><br /><br />
or a Contractor Entity or a Subcontractor;                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(b)    the breakdown or failure of any Assets caused by normal wear and tear or                                                   <br /><br /><br />
caused by the failure of the Contractor to maintain such Assets or to maintain a                                                  <br /><br /><br />
suitable stock of spares;                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
(c)    any event or circumstance affecting any third party;                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(d)    any event or circumstance which comprises or results from any wilful                                                       <br /><br /><br />
misconduct or gross negligence of the Contractor, or any act or omission by the                                                   <br /><br /><br />
Contractor which could have been prevented or overcome by the exercise by                                                         <br /><br /><br />
the Contractor of the standard of a reasonable and prudent operator acting in                                                     <br /><br /><br />
accordance with Best Practices;                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />

﻿                                                                Production Shoring Contract Dtnarta  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
(e)    the imposition of sanction* by the Government due solely to the failure of the                <br /><br /><br />
Contractor to comply with any Applicable Law;                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(f)    change of Applicable Law: and                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
(g| the inability or the failure of the Contractor to raise sufficient financing for the             <br /><br /><br />
performance of the Contractor's obligations hereunder.                                               <br /><br /><br />
*0.8 The Contractor will not be entitled to relief in accordance with this clause 40. or having      <br /><br /><br />
become entitled will cease to be so entitled, to the extent that the Contractor fails to             <br /><br /><br />
comply with the requirements of this clause 40. unless such failure would itself qualify             <br /><br /><br />
as Force Majeure.                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
40.9    The Contractor shall, to the greatest extent possible, continue to perform its obligations   <br /><br /><br />
in accordance with this Contract to the extent not prevented, impeded, or delayed by                 <br /><br /><br />
Force Majeure.                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
40.10    If Force Majeure occurs, the Contractor shall take reasonable endeavours to bring the       <br /><br /><br />
Force Majeure to an end and to resume full and proper performance of the obligation to               <br /><br /><br />
which the Force Majeure relates.                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
40.11    The Contractor shall give notice (a 'Force Majeure Estimate") to the Government at          <br /><br /><br />
each of the following times:                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
(a)    forthwith after the day (the "Relevant Day") upon which the Contractor first                  <br /><br /><br />
knew or ought reasonably to have known of the inability to perform an                                <br /><br /><br />
obligation in accordance with this Contract for which relief is sought;                              <br /><br /><br />
(b)    within 7 days from the Relevant Day and on the last day of each subsequent                    <br /><br /><br />
period of 7 days thereafter; and                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
(c)    forthwith after the Contractor anticipates that it will be able to resume                     <br /><br /><br />
performance of the covenant or obligation for which relief is sought.                                <br /><br /><br />
40.12    Each Force Majeure Estimate shall contain the Contractor's good faith best estimates of     <br /><br /><br />
the following information:                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
[a)    full particulars of and the reasons for the Force Majeure event;                              <br /><br /><br />
(b)    the expected extent of the Contractor's inability to perform any covenant or                  <br /><br /><br />
obligation in accordance with this Contract;                                                         <br /><br /><br />
[c)    the expected duration of the Force Majeure from the Relevant Day and the                      <br /><br /><br />
expected date that performance of the covenant or obligation to which the                            <br /><br /><br />
Force Majeure relates will be resumed (whether incrementally or in whole);                           <br /><br /><br />
and                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
(d)    the actions which the Contractor proposes to take to bring the Force Majeure                  <br /><br /><br />
event to an end and to resume full and proper performance of the obligation to                       <br /><br /><br />
which the Force Majeure relates and the Contractor's estimate of the expected                        <br /><br /><br />
schedule thereof.                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
40.13    The Contractor shall ensure that each subsequent Force Majeure Estimate will contain        <br /><br /><br />
any of the above information not previously given notice of. a full report confirming or             <br /><br /><br />
updating and amplifying the information contained in any previous Force Majeure                      <br /><br /><br />
Estimates and such further information as the Government may reasonably request.                     <br /><br /><br />

Contractor Entities shall appoint one arbitrator. If the parties to the Dispute are               <br /><br /><br />
the Government and one Contractor Entity, the Government and such                                 <br /><br /><br />
Contractor Entity shall each appoint one arbitrator.                                              <br /><br /><br />
42.5.5    The two arbitrators so appointed shall, in good faith, use all reasonable               <br /><br /><br />
endeavours to agree on the appointment of the third arbitrator, who will chair                    <br /><br /><br />
the arbitral tribunal. In case of failure to appoint an arbitrator or to agree on                 <br /><br /><br />
the appointment of the third arbitrator, the Rules of the LCIA shall apply.                       <br /><br /><br />
42.5.6    The seat of arbitration shall be London. England. The language to be used in            <br /><br /><br />
any prior negotiation, mediation and in the arbitration shall be English. The                     <br /><br /><br />
arbitral award may be enforced by any court of competent jurisdiction. Any                        <br /><br /><br />
award shall be expressed in US$.                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
42.5.7    The Parties agree that the arbitral award will be final and not subject to any          <br /><br /><br />
appeal, including to the Courts of England on issues of Law.                                      <br /><br /><br />

to this Contract.                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />

and signed amendments.                                                                                <br /><br /><br />

that instance and only for the purpose stated. A waiver once given is not to be                       <br /><br /><br />
construed as a waiver on any future occasion. No waiver or amendment in respect of                    <br /><br /><br />
this Contract will constitute a waiver or amendment of any other agreement or contract,               <br /><br /><br />
except as expressly set forth in such waiver or amendment.                                            <br /><br /><br />

any right or condition or any provision, right, or condition of this Contract.                        <br /><br /><br />

 Annex B                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
              Accounting Procedures                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
PARAGRAPH 1 - GENERAL PROVISIONS                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
1.1 Purpose                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
The purpose of this Annex B - Accounting Procedures is to classify expenditures, define further                  <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Costs (in addition to those defined as such in the clauses of the Contract), and                       <br /><br /><br />
prescribe the manner in which the Accounts shall be prepared and approved.                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
1.2 Definitions                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
Words and phrases to which a meaning has been assigned in clause 1 or other clauses of the                       <br /><br /><br />
Contract shall have the same meaning when used in this Annex.                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
1.3 Inconsistency                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
In the event of any inconsistency or conflict between the provisions of these Accounting                         <br /><br /><br />
Procedures and the main body of the Contract, the provisions of the main body of the Contract                    <br /><br /><br />
will control.                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
1.4 Accounting Records and Reports                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
1.4.1    The Contractor shall maintain the Accounts in accordance with clause 15 and this                        <br /><br /><br />
Accounting Procedure.                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
1.4.2    Within 60 days of the Effective Date, the Contractor shall submit to and discuss with the               <br /><br /><br />
Government a proposed outline of charts of Accounts in accordance with generally                                 <br /><br /><br />
accepted standards and recognized accounting systems and consistent with normal                                  <br /><br /><br />
petroleum industry practice and procedures.                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
1.4.5    Within 90 days of receiving the above submission, the Government shall either provide                   <br /><br /><br />
written notification of its approval of the proposal or request in writing revisions to the                      <br /><br /><br />
proposal.                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
1.4.4 Within 180 days after the Effective Date, the Contractor and the Government shall agree                    <br /><br /><br />
on the outline of charts of Accounts which describe the basis of the accounting system                           <br /><br /><br />
and procedures to be developed and used under this Contract.                                                     <br /><br /><br />
1.4.s Following such agreement, the Contractor shall expeditiously prepare and provide the                       <br /><br /><br />
Government with formal copies of the comprehensive charts of Accounts and manuals                                <br /><br /><br />
related to the accounting, recording and reporting functions, and procedures which are.                          <br /><br /><br />
and shall be, observed under the Contract.                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
1.4.6    Notwithstanding the generality of the foregoing, the Contractor shall provide regular                   <br /><br /><br />
statements relating to the Petroleum Operations:                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
(a) Production Statements (Paragraph 6);                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
(b| Value of Production and Pricing Statements (Paragraph 7);                                                    <br /><br /><br />
(c| Cost Recovery and Share Account Statements (Paragraph 8|;                                                    <br /><br /><br />
(d| Statements of Expenditures and Receipts (Paragraph 9);                                                       <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                           B- 1  <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                                                                                    Production Shoring Contract • Dinatta     <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
 (e)    final Endof-Year Statements IParagraph 10): and                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
 (f)    8udget Statements (Paragraph 12).                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
 1.4.7 All reports and statements shall be prepared in accordance with the Contract. Applicable                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
 Law. and where there are no relevant provisions of either of these, in accordance with                                                       <br /><br /><br />
 Best Practices.                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
l.S Language and Units of Account                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
All Accounts shall be maintained and prepared in the English language and shall be recorded in                                                <br /><br /><br />
US Dollars. Where necessary for clarification, the Contractor may also maintain Accounts in                                                   <br /><br /><br />
other currencies.                                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
1.6    Audit and Inspection Rights of the Government                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
The following provisions shall apply to any audit carried out in accordance with clauses 15.2 to                                              <br /><br /><br />
15.7:                                                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
1.6.1    for purposes of auditing, the Government, acting reasonably, may examine and verify,                                                 <br /><br /><br />
at reasonable times upon reasonable prior written notice to the Contractor, all                                                               <br /><br /><br />
accounting records, including charges and credits relating to the Petroleum Operations,                                                       <br /><br /><br />
such as records of account, accounting entries, supporting records and inventories,                                                           <br /><br /><br />
vouchers, payrolls, invoices and any other documents, correspondence and records                                                              <br /><br /><br />
including electronic records reasonably considered necessary by the Government to                                                             <br /><br /><br />
audit and verify the charges and credits, values and treatments.                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
1.6.2    The auditors are entitled to visit and inspect at reasonable times, all sites, plants,                                               <br /><br /><br />
facilities, warehouses and offices of the Contractor directly or indirectly serving the                                                       <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Operations and to question personnel associated with those Petroleum                                                                <br /><br /><br />
Operations.                                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
1.6.s Where the Government requires verification of charges made by an Affiliate of a                                                         <br /><br /><br />
Contractor Entity, the Government shall have the right to obtain an audit certificate for                                                     <br /><br /><br />
such changes from an internationally recognised firm of public accountants acceptable                                                         <br /><br /><br />
to both the Government and the Contractor.                                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
1.6.4 All agreed adjustments resulting from an audit shall be promptly made in the Accounts                                                   <br /><br /><br />
and any consequential adjustments to payments due to the Contractor or to the                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
Government, as the case may be. shall be made promptly.                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
1.6.4 When issues are outstanding with respect to an audit, the Contractor shall maintain the                                                 <br /><br /><br />
relevant documents and permit inspection thereof until the issue is resolved.                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
1.7    Accrual Basis. Cash Flow Basis and Reports                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
All Accounts shall be prepared on an accrual basis in accordance with generally accepted                                                      <br /><br /><br />
accounting principles used in the international petroleum industry.                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
1.8 Values and Treatments                                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
Values and treatments proposed by the Contractor relating to all Petroleum Costs shall be                                                     <br /><br /><br />
subject to challenge by the Government in the course of audit to ensure that they are in                                                      <br /><br /><br />
accordance with the provisions of this Accounting Procedure.                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                       B- 2   <br /><br /><br />
﻿                                                                                                                                      Production Shoring Contract • Dinatta    <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
PARAGRAPH 2 - COSTS ANO EXPENSES                                                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
2.1 Segregation off Costs and Expenses                                                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
2.1.1    Petroleum Costs must be segregated in accordance with the purposes ffor which such                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
Petroleum Costs are made. The purposes which Qualify are:                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
(a) those which have been included in the approved Work Program and Budget ffor                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
the year in which the Costs and Expenditures are made;                                                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
(b| expenditures incurred in cases off emergency under the Contract;                                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
(c| any other purposes agreed in the Contract; and                                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
(d| other items which have been agreed by the Government and the Contractor.                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
2.1.2    All Petroleum Costs recoverable under Paragraph 3 as Petroleum Operations shall be                                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
treated as set out in the balance off this Paragraph 2.                                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
2.2    Exploration Costs                                                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
Exploration Costs are all direct and allocated indirect costs and expenditures incurred in carrying                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
out the Exploration Operations, including all direct and allocated indirect costs and expenditures                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
incurred ;n the search for Petroleum in an area which is, or was at the time when such costs and                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
expenses were incurred, part off the Contract Area, including:                                                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
(a)    aerial, geophysical, geochemical, paleontological, geological, topographical and seismic                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
surveys and studies and their interpretation and purchased geological and geophysical                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
information;                                                                                                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
(b)    stratigraphic test hole drilling and water well drilling;                                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
(c)    labour, materials, supplies, and services used in drilling and formation testing off wells                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
with the object off finding Petroleum or Appraisal Wells excluding any costs off the                                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
subsequent completion off such wells as producing wells;                                                                                                                       <br /><br /><br />
(d)    facilities to the extent used m support of the purposes described in (a), |b), and (c|.                                                                                 <br /><br /><br />
including access roads;                                                                                                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(e)    that portion off all service expenditures and that portion off all general and administrative                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
expenditures directly attributable to Exploration Costs or allocated thereto on a                                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
consistent and equitable basis; and                                                                                                                                            <br /><br /><br />

prevailing in normal arm's length transactions on the open market and in any case                                                       <br /><br /><br />
shall not exceed a fee equal to 2% of the value of the materials added to the cost of                                                   <br /><br /><br />
the materials purchased.                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />

PARAGRAPH 6 - PRODUCTION STATEMENT                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
6.1    Production Information                                                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
Without prejudice to the rights and obligations of the Parties under clause 16 of the Contract,                                   <br /><br /><br />
from the date of First Production from the Contract Area the Contractor shall submit a monthly                                    <br /><br /><br />
production statement to the Government showing the following information separately for each                                      <br /><br /><br />
producing Development Area and in aggregate for the Contract Area:                                                                <br /><br /><br />
(a)    the quantity of Crude Oil produced and saved;                                                                              <br /><br /><br />
(b)    the quality characteristics of such Crude Oil produced and save;                                                           <br /><br /><br />
(c)    the quantity of Natural Gas produced and saved;                                                                            <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
(d)    the quality characteristics of such Natural Gas produced and saved;                                                        <br /><br /><br />
(e)    the quantities of Crude Oil and Natural Gas used for the purposes of carrying on drilling                                  <br /><br /><br />
and production operations and pumping to field storage;                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
(f)    the quantities of Crude Oil and Natural Gas unavoidably lost;                                                              <br /><br /><br />
(g)    the quantities of Natural Gas flared and vented;                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
(h)    the size of Petroleum stocks held at the beginning of the calendar Month in question;                                      <br /><br /><br />
                                                                                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
(i|    the size of Petroleum stocks held at the end of the calendar Month in question;                                            <br /><br /><br />
(j)    the quantities of Natural Gas reinjected into the Reservoir; and                                                           <br /><br /><br />
(k} in respect of the Contract Area as a whole, the quantities of Petroleum transferred at                                        <br /><br /><br />
the Measurement Point. All quantities shown in this Statement shall be expressed in                                               <br /><br /><br />
both volumetric terms (Barrels of oil and cubic meters of gas} and in weight (metric                                              <br /><br /><br />
tonnes).                                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />

13 and Applicable Law.                                                                                                                                             <br /><br /><br />

Operations to enable the Government to verify and audit Taxes payable by such Contractor Entity                                                                    <br /><br /><br />
for a tax period. Such Accounts shall be prepared and maintained on a cash or accrual basis as                                                                     <br /><br /><br />
required by Applicable Law in respect of Taxes and maintained throughout the term of the                                                                           <br /><br /><br />
Contract and for a period of five years thereafter.                                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />

entitled under clause 26; and                                                                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />

treatment, storage, or transportation of products for third parties.                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
