1.1 Definitions; Interpretation                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
1.1    Definitions                                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
1.1.1    Unless defined in this Guarantee, terms defined in the Contract have the same meaning in    <br /><br /><br />
this Guarantee.                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
1.1.2    As used in this Guarantee:                                                                  <br /><br /><br />
“Demand* is defined in clause 2.3.                                                                   <br /><br /><br />
“Government* is defined in the preamble.                                                             <br /><br /><br />
“Guaranteed Obligations* is defined in clause 2.1.                                                   <br /><br /><br />
“Guarantors*' means |X and Y| and "Guarantor" means either of |X or Y).                              <br /><br /><br />
“Person* means any individual, company, corporation, firm, partnership, joint venture,               <br /><br /><br />
association, organisation, state or agency of a state or other entity, whether or not having         <br /><br /><br />
separate legal personality.                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
1.2    Construction and Interpretation                                                               <br /><br /><br />
1.2.1    Any reference to a clause or annex is, unless otherwise stated, to a clause or annex of     <br /><br /><br />
this Guarantee.                                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
1.2.2    Any reference to a "clause* is to a "clause" of this Guarantee.                             <br /><br /><br />

2. Guarantee                                                                                         <br /><br /><br />
2.1    Guaranteed Obligations                                                                        <br /><br /><br />
The Guarantors guarantee to the Government the due and punctual payment of the Second Sub¬           <br /><br /><br />
Period Guaranteed Amount in the manner and currency prescribed by the Contract for payments          <br /><br /><br />
by the Contractor together with any interest due with respect thereto as provided in the Contract    <br /><br /><br />
(the "Guaranteed Obligations").                                                                      <br /><br /><br />
2.2    Joint and Several                                                                             <br /><br /><br />
The liability of each Guarantor under this Guarantee is joint and several. Every undertaking and     <br /><br /><br />
agreement contained in this Guarantee is to be construed as joint and several ooligatcons of the     <br /><br /><br />
Guarantors.                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />

 2.3    Demand                                                                                                <br /><br /><br />
 A Guarantor will have no obligation in respect of a Guaranteed Obligation unless the Guarantor               <br /><br /><br />
 has received a written demand for payment {the ''Demand'). The Government may submit a                       <br /><br /><br />
 Demand to either or both Guarantors. A Oemand must:                                                          <br /><br /><br />
 (a) make specific reference to this Guarantee;                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 lb) state the amount that is demanded and which components of the Guaranteed Obligations                     <br /><br /><br />
 are the subject of the Demand;                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 (c)    state that the Government has not received payment of the relevant Guaranteed                         <br /><br /><br />
 Obligation from the Contractor Entity on the date on which it became due and payable;                        <br /><br /><br />
 and                                                                                                          <br /><br /><br />
 [d)    provide the Government's wire instructions for the payment of the Demand.                             <br /><br /><br />
 2.4    Payment                                                                                               <br /><br /><br />
 A Guarantor shall make payment to the Government in accordance with a Demand by wire                         <br /><br /><br />
 transfer of cleared funds in US$ in accordance with the Government’s wire instructions within S              <br /><br /><br />
 International Business Days after receipt of a Demand.                                                       <br /><br /><br />

and not of collection, and whether by acceleration or otherwise.                                              <br /><br /><br />

a condition to, exercising any of the rights, powers, or remedies conferred upon the Government               <br /><br /><br />
by this Guarantee or by applicable law. Without limiting the generality of the foregoing, the                 <br /><br /><br />
Government will not be required to {a) take any action or obtain judgment in any court against                <br /><br /><br />
the Contractor, a Contractor Entity or any other Person, or (b) to make or file any daim or proof             <br /><br /><br />
n a winding up or dissolution of the Contractor, a Contractor Entity or any other Person.                     <br /><br /><br />
